                10.1002/smtd.201800533</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord empty" id="
                            rightTab-cas_R
                        "><div class="casContent">There is no corresponding record for this reference.</div></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref50"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref50" class="rightTabRefNumLink">50</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit50" data-doi="10.1016/j.electacta.2016.04.086"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Sun, Y.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Li, C.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Yang, Q.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Chou, S.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Liu, H.</span></span> <span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Electrochemically Active, Novel Layered m-ZnV<sub>2</sub>O<sub>6</sub> Nanobelts for Highly Rechargeable Na-Ion Energy Storage</span>. <i>Electrochim. Acta</i>  <span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2016</span>,  <span class="NLM_volume"><i>205</i></span>,  <span class="NLM_fpage">62</span>– <span class="NLM_lpage">69</span>, <span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1016/j.electacta.2016.04.086</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit50R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">50</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Electrochemically active, novel layered m-ZnV2O6 nanobelts for highly rechargeable Na-ion energy storage</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Sun, Yan; Li, Chun-Sheng; Yang, Qiu-Ran; Chou, Shu-Lei; Liu, Hua-Kun</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Electrochimica Acta</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2016</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">205</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue"></span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">62-69</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">ELCAAV</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">0013-4686</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Elsevier Ltd.</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">Electrode materials with a three-dimensional (3D) layered framework and excellent electrochem. stability can provide a new avenue for enhancing the overall performance of promising Na ion batteries.  Here, layered monoclinic (m) - ZnV2O6 nanobelts with high chem. activity for Na-ion energy storage were effectively fabricated via a rapid microwave irradn. method over the reaction time of 8 h, in which the fabricating efficiency is 24.5 times greater in comparison with the traditional hydrothermal method.  The morphol. and phase evolutions were verified by x-ray diffraction, SEM, and TEM.  This study also proposes the topotactic transformation-Ostwald ripening mechanism in layered m-ZnV2O6 nanobelts, from 1-dimensional (1D) m-Zn2V2O7 with tunnel structure to a 3-dimensional m-ZnV2O6 layered structure.  In particular, the m-ZnV2O6 nanobelt anode exhibited a high discharge capacity of 480.5 mAh g-1 at a c.d. of 10 mA g-1, and maintained the considerable discharge capacity of 246.9 mAh g-1 at the 100th cycle.  The very preliminary results are promising and confirming that layered metallic V can give a new insight into designing novel anode materials for high-efficiency energy storage in Na ion batteries.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGoM7NbkW4sqqrVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0li-ywPt4bW1MA"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC28XnsVCnsrk%253D&amp;md5=1a0b339145fa31d9687d3db62221e01f</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref51"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref51" class="rightTabRefNumLink">51</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit51" data-doi="10.1016/j.jpowsour.2019.01.033"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Nguyen, T. L.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Salunkhe, T. T.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Vo, T. N.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Choi, H. W.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Lee, Y. C.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Choi, J. S.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Hur, J.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Kim, I. T.</span></span> <span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Tailored Synthesis of Antimony-Based Alloy/Oxides Nanosheets for High-Performance Sodium-Ion Battery Anodes</span>. <i>J. Power Sources</i>  <span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2019</span>,  <span class="NLM_volume"><i>414</i></span>,  <span class="NLM_fpage">470</span>– <span class="NLM_lpage">478</span>, <span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1016/j.jpowsour.2019.01.033</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit51R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">51</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Tailored synthesis of antimony-based alloy/oxides nanosheets for high-performance sodium-ion battery anodes</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Nguyen, Tuan Loi; Salunkhe, Tejaswi Tanaji; Vo, Thuan Ngoc; Choi, Hyung Wook; Lee, Young-Chul; Choi, Jin-Seok; Hur, Jaehyun; Kim, Il Tae</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">Journal of Power Sources</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2019</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">414</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue"></span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">470-478</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">JPSODZ</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">0378-7753</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">Elsevier B.V.</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">We report a facile approach to synthesize NixSbyOz nanosheet mixts. consisting of Sb, Sb2O3 and NiSb2 for application as potential anode materials in sodium-ion batteries.  The reaction time affects the morphol., particle size, and phase components of the NixSbyOz nanosheet mixts.  The nanosheet mixt. (specifically, NixSbyOz-6h) exhibits an impressive electrochem. performance by demonstrating a remarkable cycling stability (over 250 cycles) with high coulombic efficiency (∼99%), reversible sodium storage capacity (∼382 mAh g-1), and excellent rate capability (∼315 mAh g-1 at 10 A g-1).  The notable electrochem. performance can be ascribed to the presence of layered structures and the Ni inactive phase functioning as buffer spaces for the significant vol. expansion of Sb and preventing the collapse of the electrodes during the cycling process, as well as the shorter Na+ diffusion length, improving reaction kinetics.  Furthermore, to realize a potential full-cell, the nanosheet anode is combined with a Prussian blue NaxFeFe(CN)6 as a cathode, which exhibits a notable electrochem. performance with stable and high rate capacity by achieving an energy d. of ∼150 Wh kg-1.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGpa5BY32-qY8bVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0li-ywPt4bW1MA"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC1MXhsVShs7Y%253D&amp;md5=7725682e76bd819cd02bd878672d8107</span></div></div></div></div></li><li id="rightTab-ref52"><div class="reference"><strong class="refLabel"><a href="#ref52" class="rightTabRefNumLink">52</a></strong><div class="NLM_citation references__item" id="rightTab-cit52" data-doi="10.1021/am508670z"><span><span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Usui, H.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Yoshioka, S.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Wasada, K.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Shimizu, M.</span></span>; <span class="NLM_contrib-group"><span class="NLM_string-name">Sakaguchi, H.</span></span> <span> </span><span class="NLM_article-title">Nb-Doped Rutile TiO<sub>2</sub>: a Potential Anode Material for Na-Ion Battery</span>. <i>ACS Appl. Mater. Interfaces</i>  <span class="NLM_year" style="font-weight: bold;">2015</span>,  <span class="NLM_volume"><i>7</i></span>,  <span class="NLM_fpage">6567</span>– <span class="NLM_lpage">6573</span>, <span class="refDoi">&nbsp;DOI:
                10.1021/am508670z</span> </span><div class=" links-group getFTR"><div class="getFTR__content getFTR__placeholder"></div><div class="casRecord" id="
                        rightTab-cas_cit52R"><div class="casContent"><span class="casTitleNuber">52</span><div class="casTitle"><span class="NLM_cas:atitle">Nb-Doped Rutile TiO2: a Potential Anode Material for Na-Ion Battery</span></div><div class="casAuthors">Usui, Hiroyuki; Yoshioka, Sho; Wasada, Kuniaki; Shimizu, Masahiro; Sakaguchi, Hiroki</div><div class="citationInfo"><span class="NLM_cas:title">ACS Applied Materials &amp; Interfaces</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:date">2015</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:volume">7</span>
        (<span class="NLM_cas:issue">12</span>),
    <span class="NLM_cas:pages">6567-6573</span>CODEN:
                <span class="NLM_cas:coden">AAMICK</span>;
        ISSN:<span class="NLM_cas:issn">1944-8244</span>.
    
            (<span class="NLM_cas:orgname">American Chemical Society</span>)
        </div><div class="casAbstract">The electrochem. properties of the rutile-type TiO2 and Nb-doped TiO2 were investigated for the first time as Na-ion battery anodes.  Ti1-xNbxO2 thick-film electrodes without a binder and a conductive additive were prepd. using a sol-gel method followed by a gas-deposition method.  The TiO2 electrode showed reversible reactions of Na insertion/extn. accompanied by expansion/contraction of the TiO2 lattice.  Among the Ti1-xNbxO2 electrodes with x = 0-0.18, the Ti0.94Nb0.06O2 electrode exhibited the best cycling performance, with a reversible capacity of 160 mA h g-1 at the 50th cycle.  As the Li-ion battery anode, this electrode also attained an excellent rate capability, with a capacity of 120 mA h g-1 even at the high c.d. of 16.75 A g-1 (50C).  The improvements in the performances are attributed to a 3 orders of magnitude higher electronic cond. of Ti0.94Nb0.06O2 compared to that of TiO2.  This offers the possibility of Nb-doped rutile TiO2 as a Na-ion battery anode as well as a Li-ion battery anode.</div></div><div class="moreSciFi"><a title="Retrieve detailed record, substances, reactions and more for this article from SciFinder ®" href="https://scifinder.cas.org/scifinder/view/link_v1/reference.jsf?l=BmxxGlm8wGr_obY7X6IHJrVg90H21EOLACvtfcHk0lg5KSGGE9pTHw"> &gt;&gt; More from SciFinder <sup>®</sup></a></div><span class="casRefUrl">https://chemport.cas.org/services/resolver?origin=ACS&amp;resolution=options&amp;coi=1%3ACAS%3A528%3ADC%252BC2MXkt1Ohsrk%253D&amp;md5=cffc55fbc6a621f14eb99a85685c9f7a</span></div></div></div></div></li></ol></li><li id="pane-m3" aria-labelledby="pane-m3" class="tab__pane tab__pane-suppInfo"><h2 class="supp-info-label">Supporting Information</h2><div class="article_supporting-info" id="rightTab-notes-1"><div class="article_content-header"><div class="article_content-header-row"><div class="article_content-title" tabindex="0"><h2 id="rightTab-_i11">Supporting Information</h2></div></div></div><hr><p class="last">The Supporting Information is available free of charge at <a href="/doi/10.1021/acsami.0c21676?goto=supporting-info" class="ext-link">https://pubs.acs.org/doi/10.1021/acsami.0c21676</a>.</p><ul class="NLM_list-list_type-label" id="silist"><li><p class="inline">Pore size of pure SbVO<sub>4</sub> and SbVO<sub>4</sub>/G; GCD profiles of pure SbVO<sub>4</sub> at 0.1 A g<sup>–1</sup>; average discharge specific capacity of SbVO<sub>4</sub>/G and pure SbVO<sub>4</sub> as LIB anodes at different current densities; GCD curves of pure SbVO<sub>4</sub> and SbVO<sub>4</sub>/G composite electrodes at current densities of 0.1–3.0 A g<sup>–1</sup>; CV curves of pure SbVO<sub>4</sub> electrodes in SIBs at 0.2 mV s<sup>–1</sup>; GCD profiles of pure SbVO<sub>4</sub> electrodes in SIBs at 0.1 A g<sup>–1</sup>; Nyquist plots of SbVO<sub>4</sub>/G and pure SbVO<sub>4</sub> in SIBs; and SEM images of the fully discharged SbVO<sub>4</sub>/G electrode for LIBs and SIBs after 50 cycles (<a href="/doi/suppl/10.1021/acsami.0c21676/suppl_file/am0c21676_si_001.pdf" class="ext-link">PDF</a>)</p></li></ul><p></p><div class="supInfoBoxOnFTP "><div class="sup-info-attachments"><ul><li><a class="suppl-anchor" href="/doi/suppl/10.1021/acsami.0c21676/suppl_file/am0c21676_si_001.pdf">am0c21676_si_001.pdf (403.04 kb)</a></li></ul></div></div><div id="rightTab-figshare-widget"></div><br><div class="TermsAndConditionsDropzoneRight" data-pb-dropzone="TermsAndConditionsDropzoneRight"><div data-widget-def="UX3HTMLWidget" data-widget-id="b84e6b6c-b4d0-4427-b286-3cf14d52d013" class="mb-4">

(function(){
	
	/*Event Tracking for RIS menu dropdown - Article pages*/

	$('.cit-download-dropdown_button').on('click',function(e)
	{	
		e.preventDefault();
	    gtag('event', 'Export', { 'event_category': 'Citation', 'event_label':'Main'});

	});


	$('.cit-download-dropdown_content ul li').on('click',function(e)
	{	
	//	e.preventDefault();
	    var idx = $(this).index();
	    
	    var label = '';
	    if (idx === 0 ) {
	    	label = 'Citation';
	    } else if (idx === 1 ) {
	    	label = 'Abstract';
	    } else if (idx === 2 ) {
	    	label = 'Reference';
	    } else if (idx === 3 ) {
	    	label = 'More Options';
	    }
	   
	   gtag('event', 'Export', { 'event_category': 'Citation', 'event_label':label});
	});

	$('.header_contnav-next a').on('click', function(e){
        e.preventDefault();
        gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Right Arrow'});
	}); 

 	$('.header_contnav-pre a').on('click', function(e){
	    e.preventDefault();
	     gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Left Arrow'});
	}); 

	$('.share_button').on('click', function(e){
		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Top', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Share'});
	});

	$("#pane-m1con").on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Figures'});
	});

	$("#pane-m2con").on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
	    gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'References'});
	});

	$("#pane-m3con").on('click', function(e) {
		e.preventDefault();
		gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Supporting Info'});
	});

	$('.tab__close').on('click', function(){
		gtag('event', 'Sidebar', { 'event_category': 'Article', 'event_label':'Close'});
	}); 



})();

<script nonce="90da870c2dd2b325-SJC">
    document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function(){
    // Function to get a Human readable formatted date
    function getFormattedDateForMaintenance() {
        let today = new Date();
        let dd = String(today.getDate()).padStart(2, '0');
        //January is 0
        let mm = String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0'); 
        let yyyy = today.getFullYear();
        
        let daysOfWeek = ['Sunday', 'Monday', 'Tuesday', 'Wednesday', 'Thursday', 'Friday', 'Saturday'];
        let monthsOfYear = ['January', 'February', 'March', 'April', 'May', 'June', 'July', 'August', 'September', 'October', 'November', 'December'];

        let dayOfWeek = daysOfWeek[today.getDay()];
        let monthOfYear = monthsOfYear[today.getMonth()];

        return dayOfWeek + ', ' + monthOfYear + ' ' + dd + ', ' + yyyy;
    }
    
    // Insert the date into the .system-message-date element
    document.querySelector('.system-message-date').innerText = getFormattedDateForMaintenance();
});
</script>

<script type="text/javascript" nonce="90da870c2dd2b325-SJC">

|\-|\/)|ibro|idea|ig01|ikom|im1k|inno|ipaq|iris|ja(t|v)a|jbro|jemu|jigs|kddi|keji|kgt( |\/)|klon|kpt |kwc\-|kyo(c|k)|le(no|xi)|lg( g|\/(k|l|u)|50|54|\-[a-w])|libw|lynx|m1\-w|m3ga|m50\/|ma(te|ui|xo)|mc(01|21|ca)|m\-cr|me(rc|ri)|mi(o8|oa|ts)|mmef|mo(01|02|bi|de|do|t(\-| |o|v)|zz)|mt(50|p1|v )|mwbp|mywa|n10[0-2]|n20[2-3]|n30(0|2)|n50(0|2|5)|n7(0(0|1)|10)|ne((c|m)\-|on|tf|wf|wg|wt)|nok(6|i)|nzph|o2im|op(ti|wv)|oran|owg1|p800|pan(a|d|t)|pdxg|pg(13|\-([1-8]|c))|phil|pire|pl(ay|uc)|pn\-2|po(ck|rt|se)|prox|psio|pt\-g|qa\-a|qc(07|12|21|32|60|\-[2-7]|i\-)|qtek|r380|r600|raks|rim9|ro(ve|zo)|s55\/|sa(ge|ma|mm|ms|ny|va)|sc(01|h\-|oo|p\-)|sdk\/|se(c(\-|0|1)|47|mc|nd|ri)|sgh\-|shar|sie(\-|m)|sk\-0|sl(45|id)|sm(al|ar|b3|it|t5)|so(ft|ny)|sp(01|h\-|v\-|v )|sy(01|mb)|t2(18|50)|t6(00|10|18)|ta(gt|lk)|tcl\-|tdg\-|tel(i|m)|tim\-|t\-mo|to(pl|sh)|ts(70|m\-|m3|m5)|tx\-9|up(\.b|g1|si)|utst|v400|v750|veri|vi(rg|te)|vk(40|5[0-3]|\-v)|vm40|voda|vulc|vx(52|53|60|61|70|80|81|83|85|98)|w3c(\-| )|webc|whit|wi(g |nc|nw)|wmlb|wonu|x700|yas\-|your|zeto|zte\-/i.test(a.substr(0,4))) check = true;})(navigator.userAgent||navigator.vendor||window.opera);
              return check;
        };

    var _isMobile = window.mobilecheck();
    if (_isMobile) {
        $('#gdpr-message-modal').addClass('mobile');
    }

    var emailValid = "",
        time = 3000,
        btnStatus = true,
        errorStatus = false,
        errormessage = "<p class='gdpr_err'><b>Please Enter a valid email address<b><p>";

    function init() {
        setTimeout(function() {
            var cookieExist = getCookie("gdpr");
            if (cookieExist) {
                //console.log("gdpr cookie exist");
                return false;
            } else {
                //console.log("gdpr cookie does not exist")
                gdprMessage();
            }
            //Events
            $('#closebtn').on("click", hideForm);

            //Handle submit
            $('#gdpr-message-btn').on("click", function(event) {
                handleClick();
            });

            // //Hide if clicked outside div - TO DO stop handling click after submit
            // $(document).click(function(event) {
            // 	event.stopPropagation();
            //   console.log(event.target);
            //   if (!$(event.target).closest("#gdpr-message-content").length) {
            //     $("body").find("#gdpr-message-modal").hide();
            //     $(this).off();
            //   }
            // });
            $('#gdpr-con-btn').click(function() {
                setCookie("gdpr", "true");
                hideForm();
            });
        }, time);
    }

    //Show the message
    function gdprMessage() {
        //console.log("Show GDPR Message");
        var tMessage, emailInput, messageButton, ewrap;

        $('#gdpr-message-modal').show();
    }

    function handleClick() {
        //console.log($("#gdpr-input").val());
        emailValid = validateEmail($("#gdpr-input").val());
        if (emailValid) {
            //Submit the form
            //Hide form
            if ($('.gdpr_err')) {
                $('.gdpr_err').hide();
            }

            $("#gdpr-message-content")
                //If successful then...
            setCookie("gdpr", "true");
            //console.log("emailValid " + emailValid + " submiting form");
        } else {
            //Show error message
            gdprErrorMessage();
            //console.log("emailValid " + emailValid);
        }
    }

    function gdprErrorMessage() {
        if (errorStatus) {
            return false;
        } else {
            errorStatus = true;
            $("#gdpr-message-content").append(errormessage);
        }
    }

    function validateEmail(email) {
        var re = /^(([^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+(\.[^<>()\[\]\\.,;:\s@"]+)*)|(".+"))@((\[[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\.[0-9]{1,3}\])|(([a-zA-Z\-0-9]+\.)+[a-zA-Z]{2,}))$/;
        return re.test(String(email).toLowerCase());
    }

    function setCookie(name, value) {
        var expires = "";
        expires = "; expires=Fri, 31 Dec 9999 23:59:59 GMT";
        document.cookie = name + "=" + (value || "") + expires + "; path=/";
    }

    function getCookie(name) {
        var match = document.cookie.match(new RegExp(name + '=([^;]+)'));
        if (match) return match[1];
    }

    function hideForm() { //And set cookie
        $('#gdpr-message-modal').hide();
        setCookie("gdpr", "false");
        gtag('event', 'GDPR Modal', { 'event_category': 'Pubs GDPR', 'event_label':'GDPR Dismissal'});
    }

    return {
        init: init
    }
})();

$(document).ready(infoCentralCapture.init);
</script>


                    
                        



        
        <script nonce="90da870c2dd2b325-SJC">
var currentJournal = "ACS Applied Materials &amp;amp; Interfaces";
$(".citationLinks > a").click(function(e){
    if($(this).text() === "ACS Full Text ") {
        gtag('event', 'ACS Full Text', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "Crossref") {
        gtag('event', 'Crossref', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "CAS") {
        gtag('event', 'CAS', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "PubMed") {
        gtag('event', 'PubMed', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).text() === "Google Scholar") {
        gtag('event', 'Google Scholar', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
    else if($(this).hasClass("issue-item_open-url") === true) {
        gtag('event', 'OpenURL', { 'event_category': 'Reference _Click', 'event_label':currentJournal});
    }
});
</script>

$(document).ready(function(){
    var cookie = "";
    var uri = "/doi/full/10.1021/html_original_uri?id=123";
    console.log("ACSPubs2 start");
    $.getJSON('https://extreme-ip-lookup.com/json/', function(data, status) {
            if ( status == 'success' ) {
                $.each(data, function(i, field){
                    cookie=cookie.concat(i+' = '+field+" - ");
                });
                
            } else {
                    cookie=status;
            }

            cookie1 = cookie;
            cookie = cookie1 + "; path=/; domain=.acs.org";
            //document.cookie = "ACSPubs2= "+ btoa(cookie) ;
            $.cookie("ACSPubs2", btoa(cookie), {path: '/'}); // Session cookie valid across the entire site.
            //TODO send cookie val to the controller for logging
            console.log("ACSPubs2 success");
    })
    .fail(function(xx, status, err){
        cookie="error: 127.0.0.1";
        //document.cookie = "ACSPubs2= "+ btoa(cookie) ;
        $.cookie("ACSPubs2", btoa(cookie), {path: '/'}); // Session cookie valid across the entire site.
        console.log("ACSPubs2 failed");
        //TODO send cookie val to the controller for logging
    });
});
